<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грабитель.html>граби́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grabítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грабитель.html>граби́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грабитель.html>граби́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грабитель.html>граби́телей</a></b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gràbiti</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грабить.html>гра́бить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grábitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ограбить.html>огра́бить</a></b>)
</p>

<p><b>гра́б<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> мн. lt;<a href = vnd.unilang:ж.html>ж</a> 2*agt;  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> ед. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуются</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="разговорное">разг.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 2*b <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> родительном <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>падеже́</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:грабли.html>гра́блей</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-грабл-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гравюра.html>гравю́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gravjúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гравюра.html>гравю́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гравюра.html>гравю́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гравюра.html>гравю́р</a></b>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>гра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вю́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***град.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>град</a> (6959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gradъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*greh₃d-</i> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰreh₃d-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">gruodas</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*grōda-</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">grandō</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">կարկուտ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">karkut</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">ह्रादुनि</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hrāduni</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and possibly with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grind</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>град</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́да</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">meteorology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>Град</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Grad</b> idjót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s hailing.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>volley, shower
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>град</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пуля.html>пу́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>grad</b> pulʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hail of bullets</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">градъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gradŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is a reflex of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gȏrdъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">górod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which was normally inherited by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pleophony" class="extiw" title="w:pleophony">pleophony</a>. Old Church Slavonic word shows <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/liquid_metathesis" class="extiw" title="w:liquid metathesis">liquid metathesis</a> characteristic of South Slavic area.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>град</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>гра́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-town"> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> antiquated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> town, city, used as a common city name suffix (Волгоград, Калининград, Ленинград)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">стольный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:град.html>град</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stolʹnyj <b>grad</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">capital (city)</span></div> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">modern Russian: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столица.html>столи́ца</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stolíca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***градус.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:градус.html>гра́дус</a> (3878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gradus</i>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gradi</i> (to step), from Proto-Indo-European base <b>*ghredh-</b> (to go).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:градус.html>гра́дус</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grádus</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:градус.html>гра́дуса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:градус.html>гра́дусы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:градус.html>гра́дусов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> meteorology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> degree</li>

***градусник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>градусник</a> (12948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:градус.html>гра́дус</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grádus</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b>граж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ноч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γράμματα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grámmata</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́мота</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">grámota</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́моты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́моты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́мот</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reading and writing (<i>sum of knowledge necessary to be able to read and write</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́моте</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">učítʹsja <b>grámote</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to learn to read and write</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́моте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">učítʹsja <b>grámote</b> i sčótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to learn the three Rs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́моты</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne znatʹ <b>grámoty</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be unable to read or write</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:китайский.html>кита́йская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́мота</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto dlja menjá kitájskaja grámota!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s all Greek to me!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>document
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почетный.html>почётная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́мота</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">počótnaja <b>grámota</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">honorary certificate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>patent</li>
<li>diploma</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> letter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:берестяной.html>берестяна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:грамота.html>гра́мота</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">berestjanája <b>grámota</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">birch-bark letter</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гранатомет.html>гранатомёт</a> (11120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граната.html>грана́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">granáta</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grenade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мёт</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mjót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to throw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*granica</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">graníca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́ц</a></b>)

***граничить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:граничить.html>грани́чить</a> (17537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граничить.html>грани́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">graníčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to border, to be contiguous</li>
<li>to adjoin, to abut, to neighbour on</li>
<li>to verge</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́ца</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">graníca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">грани́чный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">graníčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-гранич-</b> |  суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b> |  глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

***грань.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>грань</a> (4530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>грань</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">granĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*granь</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>грань</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">granʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>гра́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>гра́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>гра́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> face (of a polyhedron)</li>
<li>facet, side</li>
<li>border, verge, brink</li></ol>
